7d9003b91aacba77f91556a590163824838b8db0	Luc Maisonobe	Thu Nov 27 15:50:42 2008 +0000	completed implementation of EigenDecompositionImpl. The implementation is now based on the very fast and accurate dqd/dqds algorithm. It is faster than Jama for all dimensions and speed gain increases with dimensions.
